
The parity check matrix for the dual of W(3,25) minus a spread is a 25b x 
26b matrix, where b is 626.

The 1 coordinates of the first row of the circulants in the qx(q+1) rep matrix is given by \
Hrep.

The length of the code is 16276 and the check matrix has rank 
8451, so the full code has dimension 7825.

There is a generator matrix for the subcode of the form (P | id) where P is quasi cyclic 
12b x 14b matrix, whose first rows are in the matrix Pbin.

The subcode has dimension 7512 so the rate is 0.4615384615384616.
